Current Affairs Commentary

Archaeological Excavation Work and Its Contributions in the Past Two Years by Zheng Shi Xu

It is to be noted that since the discovery of "Peking Man", archaeological excavation in China has become an important contribution to Chinese academia. In recent years, news of ancient tombs being excavated in various places has been disclosed from time to time. However, these are fragmentary and scattered, making it difficult for readers to grasp the full picture. The 22nd issue of this newspaper's yearbook specially invited Mr. Li Ji to provide a comprehensive account. Now, we have commissioned Mr. Zheng to write this systematic article, which is published first for those studying this issue to read quickly.

In the past two years, China's archaeological work has indeed made significant progress and practical contributions. Taking the excavation work led by the Academia Sinica as an example, there have been as many as thirteen excavations in two years. The times are listed in a simple table as follows:

(1) April 1 to May 28, 1933: Third Excavation at Xincun, Junxian County, Henan. (2) October 20 to December 25, 1933: Eighth Yinxu Excavation. (3) October 20 to December 10, 1933: Fourth Excavation at Xincun, Junxian County. (4) October 24 to November 30, 1933: First Excavation at Anshang Village, Tengxian County, Shandong. (5) October 26 to November 30, 1933: First Excavation of the Eastern Cao Wang Tomb in Anshang Village. (6) November 15, 1933 to January 24, 1934: Third Excavation at Hougang, Anyang. (7) September 1934 to March 31, 1935: Ninth Yinxu Excavation. (8) March 15 to May 22, 1934: Fourth Hougang Excavation. (9) April 2 to June 2, 1934: Second Excavation at Houjiazhuang, Anyang / Excavation at Wuguan Village. (10) May 2 to May 17, 1934: First Excavation at Mayugou Changpocun, Gongxian County, Henan. (11) May 21 to May 29, 1934: First Excavation at Chengou Village, Guangwu County, Henan, at Aowangding.

(12) October 2, 1934: Tenth Yinxu Excavation at Houjiazhuang, still underway at the end of the year. (13) October 15 to November 15, 1934: Second Excavation in Guangwu County. During these two years of excavation, although half of it was a continuation of old work, in order to explore the distribution and contact areas of black pottery and painted pottery cultures, the organizers had a plan to investigate and excavate along the south bank of the Yellow River. The trial excavations in Gongxian County and Guangwu County, Henan, were the first step in their work. In recent years, other parties have also been interested in archaeological work, such as the Henan Antiquities Research Association, professors and interns from Shandong University, etc., all of whom have participated in the work. The results of the excavation have also made quite a few contributions to China's ancient history. Roughly speaking, three items can be obtained:

1. Clarification of the Architectural Culture of the Yin and Shang Dynasties: The foundation of Shang Dynasty architecture was discovered during the seventh excavation. In the eighth excavation, two rammed-earth building foundations were found. In addition to the stone foundations, ten copper-cast foundations were also found. Under the rammed earth, a large round pit of the cave dwelling from the Black Pottery era was discovered, and a considerable connection was made with those excavated in previous years. During the second Houjiazhuang excavation, large round caves where the Yin people lived, building foundations, rammed earth, stone foundations, earthen steps, and cellars, similar to the Yinxu in Xiaotun, were discovered. Thus, the architectural culture of the Yin Dynasty can be understood.

2. Determination of the Cultural Level of the Yin and Shang Dynasties: The Shang Dynasty was a key point in the transition from the Stone Age to the Bronze Age, which is undoubtedly confirmed by the artifacts unearthed in the past. However, within the cultural layer of the Yinxu, there are also unsmelted copper ore, broken pieces of red-fired earth, charcoal, and "General Helmet" that can be used for smelting, which can be used to estimate the method of smelting copper by the Yin people.

3. Confirmation of the Actual Distribution of Yin and Shang Culture: The cultural area of the Shang Dynasty was from the south of the Yellow River to the east to the Shandong area. Wang Guowei had already made this assumption in the past. The results of the excavations in the past two years have further proved that this statement is not wrong. Oracle bone inscriptions are unique to Yinxu, and the characters on the pottery of Chengziyai are similar in font. As for the oracle bones used for divination, they have also been found repeatedly in Chengziyai, Anshang Village, Shandong, etc., and they have all been drilled and burned, which are largely the same as those unearthed from Yinxu, and are indeed influenced by the Yin and Shang cultures. In addition, the Black Pottery culture was first discovered in Chengziyai and was unique to the Shandong area. Now, Xincun in Junxian County, Hougang in Anyang, Houjiazhuang, and Tapo Village in Gongxian County all have it. The unearthed artifacts are also the same as the lower-level culture period of Chengziyai. During the third excavation in Junxian County, a pottery kiln was also found, which was very complete. This shows the general situation of cultural exchange and distribution between the two places.

In addition, the Institute of History and Philology of the Peking Academy and the Shaanxi Archaeological Society presided over the excavation of the sites of the Xingqing Palace and Daming Palace of the Tang Dynasty in the Shaanxi Provincial Government Hall in February and March of 1934. The stone maps of the two palaces were obtained, with a relatively precise scale, which is of great benefit to the archaeological community.

Special collections of reports have been printed due to the excavation results. In 1933, there was the Gao Lutaog Collection printed by the Northwest Science Expedition. The excavation report of Chengziyai by the Academia Sinica has been announced for publication, and the excavation report of Yinxu is being sorted and edited.

At the same time, in addition to the Northwest Science Expedition and the Guangzhou Huanghua Archaeological Institute, which had been established before, the China Archaeological Society was established in Shanghai on May 14, 1933, the Shaanxi Archaeological Society was established in Xi'an in the spring of 1934, and the Archaeological Society was established in Peiping on September 1, 1934. The Archaeological Society was initiated and organized by archaeologists from the north and south. It has published a journal, three special archaeological collections, one type A and three type B of archaeological series, specifically for research work. In addition, there are two things that must be recorded: one is the proposal of Dai Chuanxian, President of the Examination Yuan, to protect ancient tombs, and the other is the order of Wang Zhaoming, President of the Executive Yuan, and Chiang Kai-shek, Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission, to protect cultural relics. For details on the exchange of letters and telegrams opposing the excavation of ancient tombs, see the 15th issue of the Yenching Journal. As for Wang Jiang's telegram, it elaborated on the work outline of the Central Antiquities Preservation Committee, hoping that the whole country would cooperate to carry forward the national spirit. On July 12, 1934, the Central Antiquities Preservation Committee was established in the Executive Yuan, and on December 17, the Rules for Mining Antiquities, the Application Form for Mining Antiquities, and the Application Form for Exporting Antiquities were passed. This implies the intention of protection in the development, which can be said to take both sides into account. It is intended that the trend of tomb robbery and the smuggling of cultural relics out of the country can be stopped in the future. All of this can promote the development of our archaeological cause.

Takahashi's Fiscal Policy Conflicts with Military Opinion

Warning Against Unlimited Investment in Manchuria

British Press Believes it Could Save Constitutional Government

(Tokyo) Finance Minister Takahashi reported on the international lending and borrowing situation last year at the cabinet meeting on the 8th, and also discussed the control of investment in Manchuria and the Manchurian Incident expenses. The Army General Staff Headquarters expressed the following opinions on this: (1) The Finance Minister is worried that investments in Manchuria have not yet yielded profits. From this point of view, he advocates large-scale investment and opposes the proliferation of uncontrolled small companies. His motivation for controlling investment differs from that of the military, so he has no choice but to oppose it. However, investment in Manchuria is a national policy, and sacrifices should be made at the beginning. (2) The Finance Minister is also worried about the inflow of funds into China and opposes the military's economic policy toward Manchuria. However, the adoption of the silver standard in Manchuria is a last resort. Occasionally, because China also adopts the silver standard, there is a slight outflow, so there is no reason to oppose the military, but countermeasures should be considered. (3) The Finance Minister opposes the continued expenditure of the Manchurian Incident expenses, but the threat from the Russian army is growing, and the reality does not allow the budget to be canceled. The Finance Minister is also worried that the huge Manchurian Incident expenses will affect international lending and borrowing relations and leak capital. This is a short-sighted observation. A person holding the post of Finance Minister must be careful in his words. (Hualian Electric, 10th)

(London) The Times recently commented on the speech made by Japanese Finance Minister Takahashi in the cabinet meeting yesterday on financial issues, saying that this speech is very important. Takahashi warned his countrymen about the difficult financial situation in Japan, but the intention of his speech is not limited to this. Takahashi is openly opposing the claims of military leaders. In recent years, it has been common for civil servants in the cabinet to become pawns of the army and navy. Due to several cases of financial corruption, Japanese public opinion is deeply dissatisfied with the political parties. On the contrary, it is happy to accept the huge military expenditure demands of the army and navy. This is partly due to a sense of fatalism and partly due to increased vanity and patriotism. National propaganda is often monopolized by active-duty soldiers who shout incessantly. This is also the case in Japan. However, recently, civil servants in the cabinet have also been preparing to criticize military policy from a financial perspective. Although the former Finance Minister Fujii eventually fell into a difficult situation, he did his best to reduce military expenditure requests and oppose the military budget during his tenure. The theory on which this military budget is based is that Japan is sooner or later in danger of war. Now that Takahashi has returned to the position of Finance Minister, although he is not as openly opposed to the military budget as Fujii, he can gain strength from his rich experience and broad international reputation, and his warnings will be more effective. It is also a tonic for the weak and incompetent Japanese party politics. (Havas Electric, 9th)

(London) The London Times today criticized the position of the Japanese budget案 in an editorial, mentioning that Japanese Finance Minister Takahashi warned the cabinet yesterday not to invest in Manchuria without limitation, saying that what is more meaningful than Takahashi's warning is that Takahashi has openly confronted the warlords. In recent years, civilian cabinet members seem to have become pawns of the military, and propaganda has become the exclusive patent of the military. Although the country is in urgent need, the politicians cannot cope with it. The statement is constantly clamoring. Although the former Finance Minister Fujii was eventually rejected, he tried his best to restrain the demands of the military. Although Takahashi has not yet taken this action, with his experience and reputation, his warning should be more powerful, or it may have a good impact on Japanese party politics, which has recently caused Japan to be in a state of great vitality. (Reuters Electric, 10th)

US Continues to Purchase Silver

But Avoid Causing Drastic Fluctuations in Silver Prices

(Washington) The Associated Press learned today that despite opposition from the Far East, the U.S. government will continue to purchase large quantities of silver bullion, but will use the lowest price, and the Treasury Department will also avoid causing drastic fluctuations in world silver prices when purchasing silver. It has been rumored that the Treasury Department's silver purchases have gradually decreased. Today, officials from the department said that Treasury Secretary Morgenthau has stated that he is determined to complete the 1934 Silver Purchase Act. Officials from the Treasury Department also stated that the silver coinage surplus item in the budget does not indicate how much silver the government will purchase. However, official circles have stated that the large-scale silver purchase plan will continue. News from Shanghai stated that the Treasury Secretary has allowed China to ease the silver purchase plan to avoid sharp increases in silver prices, and agreed to use other methods to purchase silver to avoid reducing China's silver reserves. Congressional silver faction members are still paying close attention to this. In addition, the statement that the Treasury Department has reduced silver purchases has made them want to establish a bill as soon as possible. The leaders of the faction did not hope that it would have any significant results, but at that time, their own opinions were divided, so they failed to establish a mandatory bill. (National Electric, 9th)

(Washington) Senator Pope stated today that $1.39 per ounce of silver should be the goal of the silver faction. The Treasury Department has failed to do its best to purchase silver on the world market and should continue to purchase silver at home and abroad. Pope estimated that $0.96 is the minimum silver price, and this silver price can make all silver mines profitable. He is willing to support the bill of the gold-silver ratio of sixteen to one. (National Electric, 9th)

Saar Factions Confront Each Other

Demonstration Situation is Turbulent

The Internationale and German Songs are Sung Together

Portraits of Lenin and Hitler are Hung Side by Side

The Voting Results Can Now Be Predicted

Demonstrators from opposing parties in Saarbrücken today nearly clashed, but a police detachment quickly arrived to avoid causing trouble. Members of the German Front and those who advocated maintaining the status quo in the Saar gathered at the station today to welcome some voters returning from the United States, but the guests did not arrive as scheduled. The demonstrators on both sides suddenly began to shout wildly, insulting each other, and singing the Internationale and the German national anthem. At that time, the situation was turbulent, and a conflict seemed inevitable. However, the leaders of the German Front tried their best to restrain their comrades until the police arrived.

Everything is normal on the streets here, except that a shop opened by a Marxist member displayed a portrait of Lenin. Many shops have portraits and busts of Nazi leaders in their windows, as well as Nazi slogans. Although the appearance is normal, the hearts of the people are extremely nervous. There are fake leaflets being distributed announcing that Hitler's Catholic Union has been dissolved because the union cannot be combined with the godless Communists. It is also heard that residents who advocate maintaining the status quo are also distributing fake leaflets signed by Hitler's loyal party members. Both sides are trying to confuse right and wrong to achieve their goals. The authorities are deeply worried that the ballot boxes from all over the place will be stolen en route to the central counting center on Sunday, so they have made meticulous preparations and are also preventing disruptive behavior. Today, it was heard that a special train carrying the ballot boxes will be guarded by foreign soldiers, and will be protected by motorcycle convoys, tank artillery vehicles, armed vehicles, and motorized vehicles. The result of the vote seems predictable, but it is expected that the number of votes advocating maintaining the status quo will account for between 20% and 40% of the total votes.

According to a London telecommunications report, the Manchester Guardian stated that according to the Treaty of Versailles, the League of Nations can divide the Saar according to the comparative strength of the votes, but the powers clearly want to preserve the integrity of the Saar. According to another message from London, the United Kingdom has inquired to Germany whether it would be willing to send a representative to attend the meeting of the Council of the League of Nations to discuss the results of the Saar plebiscite in the future, but it has not yet received a reply. However, all recent arrangements regarding the Saar vote have been carried out in close cooperation with Germany. According to Germany, it could have participated in the meeting of the Council of the League of Nations until October, but since the German government notified its withdrawal from the League of Nations, it has never attended any meeting of the League of Nations. (Reuters Electric, 10th)

Saarbrücken Saar residents are becoming increasingly anxious as the voting date approaches. In the past two weeks, the number of cash transfers across the border to banks in France has been increasing, reaching 100 million francs, for fear that the money will be withheld after the plebiscite. (Reuters Electric, 9th)

Saarbrücken The Saar region plebiscite will be held on January 13. However, public officials, prison inmates, and hospital patients will vote in advance on January 7, 8, and 9. A total of 1,034 votes were cast in the three days, including 480 hospital patients, 360 public officials, and 194 prison inmates. According to those who are allowed to vote in advance, it is expected that there will be 2,200 people, and hospital patients are not included. It can be seen that the number of people who actually voted is very small. (Havas Electric, 9th)

Hitler's Representative Scathingly Criticizes the French Foreign Minister

Said to be Encouraging Separatist Movements

(Berlin) Burkell, the special envoy appointed by Hitler to handle the Saar issue, gave a fiery speech at the Kaiser Palace in Bavaria today, scathingly criticizing French Foreign Minister Laval, saying that Laval encouraged the Saar separatists to believe that a second plebiscite could be held, which is an illusion. Burkell also condemned Christians for joining the Communist Party and advocating maintaining the status quo in the Saar, saying that this behavior is using the name of Christ to betray the country. Burkell finally denied the claim that detention camps would be set up after the Saar plebiscite. (Reuters Electric, 9th)

Kaiserslautern Berger, the special commissioner for the Saar region appointed by German Head of State Hitler, made a declaration to foreign journalists here today, first making optimistic comments on the popular vote to be held on Sunday, saying that "harmonious ways have been unimpeded since January 13." Berger also said that at present, people all over the world are asking who will win or lose on Sunday. If this kind of question is explored with international significance, then after the vote, no matter who wins or loses, the day the vote is completed will be the time when the competition begins, because the entire voting issue will become the focus of the competition between Germany and France from beginning to end. However, if the current real problem is considered with conscience, it is felt that the Saar problem is no longer a problem of international political competition, and after the various erroneous paths that have not been resolved before, after the Saar problem is removed from the scope of international discussion, then the so-called Saar problem is purely a German affair, because this affair can only be resolved by the Germans. Berger continued to discuss the possibility of extending the status quo after the vote. He said that this possibility is a disingenuous assumption to conceal the meaning of the vote. If the League of Nations agrees to hold a second vote in the future, the Saar Statute will be completely destroyed, because the so-called maintenance of the status quo and the term of maintenance, etc., the people of the Saar will no longer be able to ask about it, and all subsequent measures will be subject to political events outside the German border and the will of foreign governments. However, the German people in the Saar, no matter what, do not want to entrust the fate of their future to foreigners and foreign governments. Therefore, those who want to extend the status quo are aiming to permanently separate the Saar from the German homeland. (National Electric, 9th)

League of Nations Meeting Today

Dispute Between Persia and Iraq

(Geneva) The 84th session of the Council of the League of Nations is scheduled to open tomorrow. This is probably the last meeting before Japan's notice of withdrawal from the League of Nations takes effect. The future of the islands administered by Japan may be discussed after the meeting. (Reuters Electric, 10th)

(Geneva) The regular meeting of the Council of the League of Nations opened on January 11, chaired by Turkish Foreign Minister Rüştü. The first meeting is expected to begin on Tuesday of next week. There are more than 30 proposals on the agenda of this session, the most important of which are the Saar issue and the border dispute between Iraq and Persia. (Havas Electric, 9th)

(Geneva) Persia recently sent a memorandum to the League of Nations, stating its position on the Iraqi border dispute. Iraq had previously protested under Article 11, Paragraph 2 of the Covenant of the League of Nations, saying that Persia did not abide by the 1914 border agreement and wanted to obtain sovereignty over the Arab River. The Persian Foreign Minister has now told reporters that the current dispute was caused by the Anglo-Russian agreement and the 1914 border treaty that forced Persia to accept it. The above-mentioned treaty has not been accepted by the Persian and former Turkish parliaments. Iraq has since become an independent country and joined the League of Nations. Persia hopes to re-determine the border, as the Republic of Turkey did, but the Iraqi government refused to accept it. Therefore, Persia intends to take the center of the river as the boundary according to custom, and does not allow the river bank as the boundary as determined in 1914. (National Electric, 10th)

(Geneva) The Soviet government has recently paid its dues for the first quarter of 1935 to the League of Nations. This move is earlier than other countries. Rozanpei, the Soviet representative in France, has been appointed as Assistant Secretary of the League of Nations. The Soviet representatives in the various committees of the League of Nations will be appointed separately by the Council during this session. (Havas Electric, 10th)

If Germany rejoins the League of Nations, it will increase one Council seat. At the same time, one seat will also be set up in Asia, so that China has the opportunity to obtain it. On the issue of Central Europe, the two governments unanimously believe that the obligation of all countries to reaffirm their respect for the independence and integrity of other countries' territories is a principle advocated by both countries. This principle is sufficient to develop the sentiment of trust among the countries in the Central European region. Soviet Russia Doubts the Strength of the Franco-Italian Agreement

Claiming that it is not yet fully resolved

(Moscow) Izvestia commented on the Franco-Italian agreement, stating: "Have France and Italy truly reached a complete agreement? Currently, information from Rome has not provided a definitive answer to this question. Although the two countries have a protocol proving their complete agreement, it cannot be said that they have a complete understanding, as such general statements have no practical effect on any country. In the protocol on Austria, France and Italy express their willingness to maintain Austria's independence and state that they will consult if Austria's independence is threatened in any way. If this protocol is limited to this and contains no more concrete content, then people will ask, 'Did France and Italy not want to maintain Austria's independence before this? Did they not consult when Austrian fascists attacked?' The whole problem lies in the following: If Austria is in danger, will France and Italy act in unison? If this understanding is not completed, then the Rome Agreement will neither enhance Austria's security nor benefit the security of other relevant countries. As for inviting other countries to join, we believe that all of Austria's neighbors except Germany can agree. We even believe that Germany itself has no reason not to join on the issue of Austria's independence. The road to hell is paved with grand statements. Without serious guarantees and without practical action to fulfill what is said, there can be no peace in Europe. The Rome negotiations, as the British press has said, are a manifestation of creating some favorable conditions for building a bridge between France and Germany. British diplomats are working in this direction. This is nothing more than obtaining a moderate amount of rhetoric and documents from the German side and allowing Germany the legal right to expand its military." Izvestia stated that the Soviet Union is always willing to solve general problems through cooperation and is willing to conclude the Eastern Regional Pact, which can consolidate the security of the people of Eastern Europe. Other regional issues must also be resolved in this way. At the same time, only agreements that strictly stipulate the rights and obligations of the participants have weight. If the Rome Agreement can indeed meet these requirements, then Moscow will support it. (TASS, 9th)

The Disarmament Issue is Raised Again

Paris newspapers discuss the matter extensively

(Paris) The disarmament issue, which has been dormant for a long time, has now been raised again due to the talks between France and Italy, becoming a topic of heated discussion. Paris newspapers have recently reported on the issue. According to Le Journal's observation, Foreign Minister Laval's actual views are quite inconsistent with France's tough note of April 17 last year. According to Mr. Laval's opinion, the danger of Germany's rearmament cannot be eliminated merely by declaring it illegal, nor can it be eliminated merely by ignoring it. Le Journal further confirmed that there was a clear intention in the Rome talks to issue another note to Germany, with the aim of requesting Germany to announce its actual military strength to the major powers in accordance with the spirit of the Five-Power Common Declaration of December 11, 1932. Only then will the major powers be prepared to recognize Germany's rearmament as legal. However, Germany must still agree to sign an international disarmament treaty. Le Journal further stated that Foreign Minister Laval intends to visit Berlin, but the date has not yet been considered. In addition, Le Matin carried a London dispatch, stating that it is quite possible that future disarmament treaties will be based on the following points: (1) Management of the arms trade, (2) Organization of a permanent disarmament committee, (3) Manufacture and application of controlled chemical weapons, (4) Major powers announce military budgets. U.S. Senate Foreign Relations Committee Approves Participation in the International Court of Justice

Abandoning the traditional policy of isolation

Democratic Senators Request the Expulsion of Foreign Nationals

(Washington) The Senate Foreign Relations Committee today voted in favor of the United States joining the Hague International Court of Justice. This move is of great significance to the future of submitting international legal disputes to arbitration, as today's resolution is tantamount to abandoning the policy of isolation adopted by the United States after President Wilson's departure in 1920. However, the Foreign Relations Committee included reservations in this resolution, one of which is aimed at protecting the United States from being bound by advisory opinions. The reservation states that the United States may join the International Court of Justice, but with the clear understanding that the International Court of Justice shall not, without the opposition of the United States, accept any request to issue an advisory opinion on any dispute or issue related to the United States. (Reuters, 9th)

(Washington) Texas Democratic Congressman Dies recently introduced a bill requesting the government to immediately deport the millions of foreign nationals who have illegally immigrated to the United States, stating that there are currently as many as seven million foreign nationals residing in the United States who have not become U.S. citizens. Expelling these people could remedy the unemployment problem. (Havas, 9th)

Lindbergh Kidnapping Case Resumes Trial, Doctor Testifies in Court

Narrating the Circumstances of Paying the Ransom

His Eloquent Delivery Captivates the Audience

Flemington: The Lindbergh kidnapping case resumed trial today. Dr. Condon, who handled the payment of the ransom, testified in court, recounting the event of handing over the ransom of $50,000 to the kidnapper in the cemetery at night, identifying Hauptmann as the person who received the ransom. Dr. Condon recounted the situation at the time, gesturing as he spoke, like a talented actor on stage, captivating the audience, who forgot that they were in court. Dr. Condon spoke for two hours and forty-five minutes, stating three times that the recipient of the money was Hauptmann. Hauptmann's face turned pale upon hearing this, but he glared at Condon, who did not flinch and glared back. Condon's testimony began by stating that the defendant claimed to be John and that he was indeed the person who received the money in the cemetery. Condon first placed an advertisement in a newspaper, using the pseudonym Jafsie to notify the kidnapper that Lindbergh's request could be accepted. He then met this John in the cemetery, talking for an hour and fifteen minutes. During the conversation, John occasionally heard sounds nearby and would jump over the fence and flee in panic, and Condon would follow him. John later calmed down slightly and said, "This is too dangerous. It's either 25 years in prison or being burned to death." By "burned to death," he meant the electric chair. At that time, Condon told him that if John cooperated, he would definitely do his best to help, otherwise he would have to follow him, even to the ends of the earth. He asked John to show him Lindbergh's child, but John refused. Finally, John sent the child's sleeping suit. Condon opened the package and inspected it in front of Lindbergh. Condon said to John in the cemetery at night, "You seem to have the beginning of a lung disease. I can give you medicine now." This statement by Dr. Condon will be a point of contention for the defendant's lawyers, as Hauptmann claims that the banknotes he obtained were given to him by Fisch, who has now died of tuberculosis in Germany. (Reuters, 9th)

U.S. Should Apologize and Compensate for the Sinking of the Can Private Smuggling Vessel

(Washington) The case of the U.S. Customs vessel sinking the One Man, a vessel transporting smuggled alcohol, in 1929 has been in litigation for many years. Today, the U.S.-Canada Mixed Commission ruled that the United States should apologize for the incident and pay $25,000 in compensation. The shipowner should not receive compensation, but the crew should not have been subjected to the harsh treatment of being thrown into the sea and imprisoned. Therefore, the United States must compensate the captain $7,906 and the remaining seven crew members each receive compensation ranging from $965 to $1,323. The family members of the drowned crew member should receive $10,185 in compensation. (Reuters, 9th)

Immigrate to agricultural areas for farming and grazing

(London) According to the Daily Telegraph, the government is currently drafting a large-scale plan to relocate industrial unemployed people to sparsely populated agricultural areas. It is estimated that 18,000 households should be resettled, divided into 115 to 20 groups. The area occupied by each group should not exceed 2 hectares. Severe Cold Grips Europe and America

(London) After the relatively warm weather of Christmas and New Year, Europe and North America are now suffering from severe cold. There is snow and ice throughout the United Kingdom, and London is shrouded in thick fog, hindering air and other transportation. It is reported that there are heavy snowstorms in continental Europe. Even Cannes, which is known for its warm weather, has had light snow in the past two days. New York Harbor has rare heavy fog, causing 13 postal ships to delay their departures by several hours. The Black Sea has experienced strong winds for three days, and several ships have sent out distress signals. (Reuters, 10th)

Bucharest, Romania: The weather is extremely cold throughout Romania, resembling the climate of Siberia. In some places, the temperature has dropped to 30 degrees Celsius below freezing. Packs of hungry wolves roam the countryside, searching for food, often attacking farmhouses and even entering villages. (Havas, 10th)

Japan's Military Budget Ranks First in the World

More than doubled compared to before the September 18th Incident

(Washington) The Foreign Policy Association recently announced that the military expenditures of major countries are higher than in the year before the European War. Since the outbreak of the Manchurian Incident in the Far East in the autumn of 1931 until the Nazi Party took power in Germany in the spring of 1933, the military strength of major countries has expanded significantly. According to the latest budgets for the navy, army, and air force announced by major countries, France's military expenditure has increased by 25.8% compared to 1913, Italy by 26.3%, the United Kingdom by 48.8%, the United States by 190.9%, and Japan by 388%. Since the Manchurian Incident in 1931, Japan's military expenditure has more than doubled. As for Germany, its military strength lags behind because Germany is still legally restricted by the Treaty of Versailles. (National Telegram, 9th)

Hungary's Revisionist Claims

Budapest: Hungary recently expressed its opinion on the agreement established by France and Italy in Rome in a semi-official manner. On the one hand, it expressed happiness for the Franco-Italian consultation, and on the other hand, it hoped that Germany could also join in order to establish effective cooperation in Europe. It also believed that the Rome Agreement did not exclude the advocacy of peaceful treaty revision. Therefore, Hungary's goal of revising the treaty is not hindered by it. Hungary's goals for revising the treaty can be summarized in three points: (1) Correct the existing borders based on history and ethnicity; (2) Equality of rights, especially with regard to national defense; (3) The rights of Hungarian minorities in foreign countries must be guaranteed. Manchester Chamber of Commerce Publishes Report on Trade with China

China's purchasing power has decreased in recent years

Japanese commercial competition remains fierce

(London) The Manchester Chamber of Commerce today released its annual report on British trade with China, which includes the statement that China is more stable, but the level of trade has decreased. It also stated that the decrease in purchasing power is the main reason for the rapid decline in the Lancashire textile trade. It is not known how the current situation can be improved until China can sell its products at better prices domestically or until the demand for its products increases. Japanese competition remains fierce, especially due to its proximity to China and convenient transportation. However, Japan's export trade is also decreasing. It continued, stating that frequent changes in Chinese tariffs force buyers to be more cautious, and that as trade decreases, tax revenue also decreases, and the high tax rates currently in place encourage large-scale smuggling. (Reuters, 10th)

Russian and Puppet Regime Waterway Conference

Both sides compete for Heixiazi Island

Technical Committee Suspends Operations

Border disputes arise frequently

Hualian News Agency, Harbin Correspondence: The Russian-puppet waterway conference was suspended on December 27, old calendar, after Russia responded to the puppet regime's request to hold a meeting at Daheihe on January 9 of last year. During that period, there were 14 consultations. On September 4, the two sides reached a waterway agreement. The representatives for the consultations were Mokhanenko, director of the shipping bureau for the Russian side, and Horiuchi, director of general affairs of the puppet navigation administration bureau for the puppet side. After the Russian-puppet waterway agreement, river disputes decreased slightly, and both sides were prepared to set boundary markers. However, regarding the delta at the confluence of the Heilongjiang and Ussuri Rivers (named Heixiazi Island), the Russian side insisted that it belonged to Russia, while the puppet side insisted that it belonged to the puppet regime. The Russian side also set up markers, prohibiting the puppet regime from navigating the northern side of the island, and built an airfield on the island, deploying Red Guards, indicating a firm unwillingness to abandon it. The puppet side repeatedly protested, but the Russian side ignored it. The joint technical committee for waterway consultation also formally requested the Russian side to withdraw the markers on December 22. The Russian committee member insisted that it belonged to Russian territory, causing the committee to suspend operations. Heixiazi Island is only 4.5 kilometers away from the Soviet military stronghold of Boli and has an area equal to Iki and Tsushima in Japan. If it is occupied by the Japanese and puppet regime, it will pose a huge threat to Boli, making the dispute difficult to resolve.

(Tokyo) Nagaoka, deputy consul of the Japanese Consulate General in Harbin, reported the following border disputes between Russia and the puppet regime to the Ministry of Foreign Affairs today: (1) Regarding the ownership of Heixiazi Island at the confluence of the Heilongjiang and Ussuri Rivers, the Russian side firmly insisted that it belonged to Russian territory based on the Sino-Russian Treaty of 1860, making it impossible to resolve the dispute. (2) On December 22 last year, the Russian side claimed that four Russian soldiers were kidnapped by puppet soldiers 7 kilometers east of Xingkai Lake. (3) On December 29, six Koreans were kidnapped by Russian soldiers in the eastern border area. In view of the continuous border disputes, the Ministry of Foreign Affairs wants to establish a Russian-Japanese-puppet border investigation committee or a border adjustment committee as soon as possible to determine the boundaries. (Hualian Telegram, 10th)

Han Fuqu Inspects Party Members Regarding the Zhang Case

The Bullets Found in Zhan Juncen's Possession Are the Same as Those Used to Assassinate Zhang

Li Wenzhai, Zhan Juncen, and Several Others Have Been Temporarily Detained

Jinan Correspondence: Since Zhang Weicun was assassinated on the evening of the 2nd, Han Fuqu, Chairman of the Provincial Government, immediately ordered the military police to strictly apprehend the murderer. For several days, there has been no progress. Han believed that Zhang had some disputes with party members before his death, and Zhang also served as a Director of Anti-Communist Special Commissioner and worked in the Special Affairs Office (i.e., the Communist Arrest Team). Thus, it was necessary to pay attention to the Special Affairs Office staff. At 9 a.m. today (the 7th), Han, in his capacity as a Standing Committee Member of the Provincial Party Headquarters, led two companies of pistol troops to the Provincial Party Headquarters. Those accompanying him included Wang Shiqi, Director of the Jinan Public Security Bureau, Shi Jingzhou, Director of the Military Law Department of the Headquarters, Lei Taiping, Adjutant General, and Yu Fengjun, Battalion Commander of the Pistol Brigade. They guarded the gates of the Provincial Party Headquarters, the doors of all offices, and the telephone room, prohibiting entry and exit and cutting off communication. Then, they summoned all staff members to give a speech in the auditorium, stating, "Fellow comrades, today is the first time I have met you all in the 24th year of the Republic. Looking back at everything that has happened in the past 23 years, although I personally hold the position of Chairman of the Shandong Provincial Government, I also rely on everyone's efforts. Therefore, although I dare not say that all achievements are good, they are generally acceptable. Unfortunately, something like what happened to Comrade Zhang has occurred, and I believe everyone is very sad and heartbroken. Since I took office as Chairman in the 19th year, I have a nature that is not good at socializing, and I do not know many people in this province. I am also a soldier with limited political ability. However, I am confident that I stand on the people's side and act entirely in the interests of the country. Regardless of which civil servant, as long as I see them as working hard for local affairs, I want to bring them together to work. I am not necessarily looking for anyone in particular to do it. I hope all comrades will continue their past efforts and add even more effort. As for Comrade Zhang's matter, it came suddenly, and we must express our feelings in order to show everyone's sincerity. Today, we must inspect everyone who has family members to see if there are any firearms or suspicious documents. I think everyone has been with Comrade Zhang for a long time, and it does not seem that there would be any ill feelings. However, there are many external discussions, and I have received many reports and letters in recent days, so it is necessary to inspect. This matter appears to have happened suddenly, but in fact, it was done by a portion of people, not just one or two people, and it must have taken one or two months of planning and a lot of thought. It is easy to find the traces, so it should not be difficult to solve." He immediately asked Zhan Juncen, the Director of the Special Affairs Team, how many people were in the Communist Arrest Team and whether they had guns. Zhan reported that there were eleven team members in total, two of whom were on leave. The team had no guns, and when they needed guns, they asked Zhang Weicun for them, because he was the Anti-Communist Special Commissioner. Next, Li Wenzhai, a Standing Committee Member, gave a speech, stating, "Comrade Zhang Weicun has been very diligent in the past for the central government and the local area. Unfortunately, he lost his life. We feel very helpless about the Party Headquarters' affairs. No matter what, we must continue to do what Comrade Zhang himself did or what he helped the government do, and we must help the government solve the case and pay attention to everyone's words, actions, and attitudes at all times. As for the Party Headquarters itself, we will never lightly trust anyone or handle anything lightly in the future. Everything must be discussed with Chairman Han." After the speeches, he ordered everyone present to write down their addresses. Anyone who had firearms or keys also handed them over at the same time. Han then sent Wang Shiqi, Shi Jingzhou, Lei Taiping, Yu Fengjun, etc. to search each house according to the addresses, while also inspecting inside the Provincial Party Headquarters. Han also studied methods with Li Wenzhai, Zhang Zhuxi, and others in the Standing Committee office. It is said that Zhan Juncen, Director of the Special Affairs Team, had conflicts with Zhang Weicun over authority and finance in the past. The central government sent someone to Jinan to mediate, so Han paid close attention to Zhan. While Han inspected each staff member, he also prepared ten tables of banquets to entertain them. Regarding those who had firearms, Li Wenzhai had one, which was taken out of his house. Qin Qirong, an Executive Committee Member, had one, but it was not found in his house. Later, Qin's gun was taken out from the house of a teacher named Sun at Zhengyi Middle School. Liu Xinwo, an alternate Executive Committee Member, had one, but his wife, having heard the news in advance, took the gun elsewhere out of fear, and it was not found. Zhan Juncen initially said he had one, but his family said he had two, but he handed over one (with one bullet still in the gun). The other one was beside a Special Affairs Team member named Xu Xiandeng, who later handed over the gun. In total, four guns were obtained. Also, eighty-two bullets (three full boxes of seventy-five and seven loose) were found in Zhan Juncen's home, which were the same as the bullets found beside Zhang Weicun after his death, which is noteworthy. However, according to Zhan, the central government had previously sent three notices instructing Zhang Weicun to pay attention and guard against communist assassinations. Zhang Weicun had also seen these notices, but unfortunately, he did not take precautions, which led to this disaster. Also, Li Zijia, a County Magistrate Training Class member, said he had a gun, but when they went to his house to look for it, his family said that the gun was at his home in Anhui. Because Li was on good terms with Zhang Weicun before his death, his mind was sometimes confused, and he just said it casually, but the gun was not actually in Jinan. After the inspection, all firearms, bullets, letters, etc. were first transported to the Military Law Department of the Headquarters. Han Fuqu went to the auditorium to report to all staff members about the inspection process, stating, "The evil trend of assassination should never be allowed to start. Moreover, Comrade Zhang held three important positions as a Central Committee Member, a Provincial Executive Committee Member, and a member of the Provincial Government. After being assassinated, the whole country is paying attention. If the case is not solved quickly, it would be too outrageous. I have no confidence in how far this case will go in the future, but we must work hard to handle it. Anyone who is slightly suspicious must be investigated, because without doing so, the case cannot be solved. I personally have too little experience in party affairs and am too busy. I have done too little to fulfill my responsibilities to the party in the past. Now that this incident has occurred, and I have been appointed as a Standing Committee Member, I cannot continue as before. In the future, all documents and matters must be notified to me by the secretariat every Tuesday and Friday. Otherwise, no matter will be allowed to proceed." After the report, he ordered those with firearms and members of the Special Affairs Team to be sent to the Military Law Department and the Public Security Bureau for temporary detention, respectively. The remaining personnel were allowed to return home, and he returned to the Provincial Government, by which time it was already 4:30 p.m. In the evening, he interrogated those involved and sent Shi Jingzhou, Director of the Military Law Department, Sun Xifeng, Deputy Director, and others to inspect the letters found in various places. The temporarily detained personnel, Li Wenzhai, Qin Qirong, and Liu Xinwo, were treated very well in the Jinan Public Security Bureau. Zhan Juncen, Director of the Special Affairs Team, and team members Wang Buyun, Tong Meng, Xu Xiandeng, Li Zhiying, Tang Heting, Ma Dewen, Cao Zhongsan, and Ma Zongying, were at the Military Law Department. The team members on leave, Xu Yiming and Ji Qingyuan, were not present. Gao Yunqing, Xu Zicai, and Zhang Yunxian were being summoned for interrogation separately. (7th)

Further Interrogation: After searching the homes of party members on the 7th in connection with the assassination of Zhang Weicun, Li Wenzhai, a Standing Committee Member of the Provincial Party Headquarters, Qin Qirong, an Executive Committee Member, and Liu Xinwo, an Alternate Executive Committee Member, were temporarily detained at the Public Security Bureau, while Zhan Juncen, Director of the Special Affairs Office, and twelve others were taken to the Military Law Department. Li, Qin, and the others were treated very well at the Public Security Bureau and had not yet been questioned. Zhan Juncen was questioned in detail one by one after arriving at the Military Law Department on the 7th, and it is said that there were many suspicious points that could be studied. At 6 a.m. yesterday (the 8th), Han Fuqu ordered Liu Shuxiang, Chief of Staff of the Headquarters, Wang Shiqi, Director of the Provincial Public Security Bureau, Sun Baofeng, Deputy Director of the Military Law Department of the Third Route Army, and Liu Yaoting, Captain of the Special Investigation Team, to be responsible for investigating the entire case. After receiving the order, Liu and others began interrogating Zhan Juncen and his team members Wang Buyun, Tong Meng, Xu Xiandeng, Li Zhiying, Tang Heting, Ma Dewen, Cao Zhongsan, Ma Zongying, Gao Yunqing, Xu Zicai, and Zhang Yunxian in the Staff Office from 9 a.m. yesterday (the 8th), took a break for lunch at 12 p.m., continued the interrogation at 1 p.m., and took a break for dinner at 5 p.m. After dinner, they continued the interrogation and also brought in a deaf person for questioning. All the confessions cannot be published because the case is important. However, regarding Zhan Juncen, there are several points that can be studied: (1) Zhan had clashed with Zhang Weicun several times last year (because Zhang was the Anti-Communist Special Commissioner and Zhan was the Director of the Special Affairs Office). The central government sent Liu to Jinan to mediate and allocate authority and finance. Zhan had returned to Nanjing once during this period. (2) Zhan's gun and bullets were the same caliber as the bullets that assassinated Zhang. Even if the caliber is the same, it is not enough to prove anything. However, Zhan's gun had fresh gunpowder residue, proving that it had been recently used, and there was only one bullet at the top of the chamber. According to Zhan's gun, it was a Browning eight-sound pistol. It can also be proved from the bullet casings that assassinated Zhang that the gun used to assassinate Zhang was an eight-sound pistol. Zhang was shot five times and an attendant was shot once, a total of six bullets. Although an eight-sound gun can hold eight bullets, an average of seven bullets are loaded. Also, when Zhan was initially questioned at the Provincial Party Headquarters on the 7th, he said that the Special Affairs Office had no guns and had to ask Zhang Weicun for them when they needed them. When an order was issued for an inspection, he stated that he had one gun. When checking his house, his family said there were two guns. As a result, one gun was found in his house and another gun was found in the Special Affairs Office. (3) Zhan initially said that there were eleven Special Affairs Team members, but later changed it to fourteen. Also, Zhang was assassinated on January 2nd, but Ji Qingyuan and Xu Yiming happened to take leave and return to the south on December 29th and 31st, respectively. They have not returned even after their leave has expired. Ji and Xu came from Nanjing with Zhan. Zhan claimed that at the time of the incident, he was watching a play at the Oriental Theater in the commercial district with Special Affairs Team members Tong Meng, Xu Xiandeng, and Wang Leyun. Wang and Tong also came from Nanjing with Zhan.

The above are the suspicious points seen by the interrogators. It is still unknown what evidence Zhan has to refute them. In short, Zhang's case is still under investigation and a definite judgment cannot be made. (9th)

Philippine House of Representatives Passes Retail Trade Restriction Act

Foreign Retailers Required to Close Down

A Major Blow to Overseas Chinese in the Philippines

Xiamen Correspondence: There are more than 140,000 overseas Chinese in the Philippines, most of whom are engaged in business, especially retailers, who occupy a very dominant position and almost control the Philippine market. Filipinos cannot compete, so there has long been a proposal to restrict retailers and prevent foreigners from engaging in the retail business. Recently, Philippine Congressman Li Aokeluo proposed a bill to restrict foreign retailers, which has been passed by the House of Representatives. The original bill stipulates that retailers in the country must have at least 75 percent of their capital owned by Filipinos or Americans in order to operate. Existing foreign retail businesses must close down by December 31, 1936. If this bill is passed by the Philippine Senate and approved by the Philippine Governor-General, it will become law and will be a major blow to our overseas Chinese retailers in the Philippines. The original bill is translated as follows: Article 1: Only American and Filipino citizens have the right to engage in retail business in the Philippines. No foreigner may engage in retail business in the Philippines. If it is a joint venture established by shareholders, at least 75 percent of the shares must be owned by Americans and Filipinos in order to be allowed to operate. Article 2: Foreign stores currently engaged in retail business in the Philippines may continue to open and sell goods until the store's inventory is exhausted after the implementation of this bill, but the period shall not exceed December 31, 1936. Article 3: Any foreigner engaged in retail business who does not comply with the provisions of Article 1 shall be deemed to be in violation of the law and shall be subject to imprisonment for one to three years. Article 4: This bill shall take effect from the date of its approval. (7th)

Xu Fu Inspects the Finances of Various Counties in Southern Fujian

Invited by Jiang Dingwen to Plan the Reconstruction of Bandit Areas

Xiamen Correspondence: Xu Fu, a member of the Fujian Provincial Government, Director of Finance, and Special Commissioner of Fujian Finance, came to Xiamen from the province with Pacification Director Jiang Dingwen and arrived here on the 4th. Xu's mission is: (1) to inspect the finances of various counties in Zhangzhou and Quanzhou in southern Fujian; (2) to negotiate the promotion and sale of short-term provincial bonds; (3) to investigate old debts owed by the provincial government. It is scheduled to go to Zhangzhou with Jiang today (the 7th). Whether to go to western Fujian for inspection will be decided upon arrival in Zhangzhou. If time is limited, they will return to the province by land from Quanzhou. According to Li Yushu, Xu's attendant, Xu's trip was at the invitation of Director Jiang to go south together. Because the reconstruction, transportation, finance, and post-disaster relief in the areas recovered from bandits need to be organized and planned, it is necessary to personally inspect and consult with local people. Although the province's finances are currently extremely stretched, military and political expenses can still be maintained completely. Xu manages the province's finances based on income and expenditure, and on the one hand, he reduces expenditures and increases revenue, so he can cope with ease and there is no so-called year-end difficulty. The current issuance of 900,000 provincial short-term bonds is a type of very short-term marketable securities with a term of nine months, and the principal and interest are repaid monthly, using the province's slaughter tax as collateral. It has been passed by the Legislative Yuan and has a very short term and collateral. Merchants can use it as marketable securities to borrow cash from banks. As for investigating the debts accumulated by previous finance directors of the provincial government, although there is currently a proposal, it is still a second step issue. (7th)

International Commercial Telegram

Special Commercial Intelligence Telegram from Reuters on January 10

Gold and Silver

London Gold: Today, the price of gold in London fell sharply. The opening price was 141 shillings and 4.5 pence, which was 6.5 pence lower than yesterday. This price drop was mostly due to the stability of the British pound.

London Silver Bars: Today's silver price, spot price is 24 pence and 0.5625, futures price is 24 pence and 0.6875, both the same as yesterday. This morning, the United States bought in again, while speculators were engaged in both buying and selling.

Bombay Silver Bars: The closing spot price in the Bombay silver market this afternoon was 64 rupees and 15 annas, up 4 annas. 15 bars were traded.

Exchange Rates

British-American: Today's foreign exchange market in London can be described as stagnant. Except for slight changes at the opening, prices remained unchanged. The opening British-American exchange rate was 4 yuan, 9 jiao, 2 fen, and 0.4375, which was 0.1875 lower than yesterday's closing British-American exchange rate. This price did not rise or fall until 2 p.m.

British-French: The opening price was 74 francs and 40, which was six pounds higher than yesterday's closing price. It has not moved since then.

Cotton and Wheat

American Cotton: The New York cotton market was slightly active. Purchases by domestic colleagues absorbed a small amount of liquidations and hedging. The opening price rose by three pounds, but there was not much change afterwards.

Indian Cotton: The Bombay cotton market rose initially due to purchases by futures traders, but then fell due to hedging and liquidations. The closing price for the Bai Luo cotton for delivery in April and May was 244 rupees and 25, which was half a rupee lower than yesterday's closing price.

British Cotton: At 1 p.m. in the Liverpool cotton market, the price for May delivery was 6.86, down two pounds.

British Wheat: The price for May delivery in the Liverpool wheat market was 5 shillings, 2 pence, and 0.25 after 1 p.m., down 0.125.

American Wheat: The Chicago wheat market opened with a slight increase due to purchases from Liverpool, and flour mills also had a slight demand in the Canadian market.

Rubber

London: The London rubber market is still sluggish. This morning's price was 6 pence and 0.875, the same as yesterday's closing price. The atmosphere is still stable.

New York: The New York rubber market did not move at the opening and was as stable as the London market. Although there was a slight buying trend within the first hour after the opening, the price rose slightly, but trading was very quiet.

Securities

New York: Wall Street seems to be trending into the same state as at the end of the year, that is, stagnant, uneven, and uninteresting. The opening of securities today has this situation, and speakers all expect the market to become even more sluggish. The opening prices are similar to yesterday's closing prices, with slight increases and decreases. There are no general news that can influence the market. Although the commercial climate is expected to be better and industries also have news of continued progress, market sentiment is not boosted by this. There must be new excitement to boost the market. The prices are as follows:
